</span>The company has the benefit of<a></a> leases which provide an income stream which the directors\nforecast will enable it to meet<a></a> its obligations as they fall\ndue for a period of not less than 12 months from the signing<a></a>\ndate of the financial statements.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>In\naddition, as a member of the Canary Wharf Group, the<a></a> company\nhas access to considerable resources.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span company will\nhave adequate resources to continue its operations for the foreseeable future.<a></a> Accordingly they continue to adopt the going concern basis in\npreparing the financial<a></a> statements.</span></p></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">As a member of the Canary Wharf Group the key\nrisks facing the company include<a></a> the cyclical nature of the\nproperty market, financing risk and concentration risk.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Cyclical Nature of the Property\nMarket</span></b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The valuation of the Canary Wharf Group's\nassets is subject to many external economic and<a></a> market\nfactors.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The turmoil in the financial\nmarkets in recent years has been reflected in the property market by such\nfactors as a significant decline in tenant demand for space in <span style=\"background:white;mso-highlight:white\">London</span>, the oversupply of\navailable space in the office market and changing market perceptions of\nproperty as an investment resulting in fluctuations in property valuations in\ngeneral.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Fears of an oversupply of\navailable space in the market have however been mitigated by the difficulty in\nsecuring finance for speculative development and reduced demand. The market has\nalso been assisted by the continuing presence of overseas investors attracted\nby the relative transparency of the real estate market in London which is\nviewed as both stable and secure. Changes in financial and property markets are\nkept under constant review so that the company can react appropriately and\ntailor its business accordingly.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>While\nthe company has no direct exposure to the Euro, the ongoing uncertainty\nreflecting issues in the macroeconomy, particularly relating to the Eurozone,\ncontinues to impact the real estate market.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>The impact of these uncertainties is closely monitored.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Financing Risk</span></b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The broader economic cycle inevitably leads\nto movements in inflation, interest rates and<a></a> bond yields.\nThe company finances its operations largely through surplus cash and<a></a> intercompany finance.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>The ongoing uncertainty in financial markets continues to<a></a>\nsignificantly limit the availability of funding. In common with other UK\nproperty<a></a> companies, lack of financing facilities may have an\nimpact on the business of Canary Wharf<a></a> Group if the lending\nmarkets remain limited for the foreseeable future.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span company, are\ncurrently located on or adjacent to the Canary Wharf Estate with a majority of<a></a> tenants linked to the financial services industry.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Wherever possible steps are taken to<a></a> mitigate or avoid material consequences arising from this\nconcentration and to diversify<a></a> the tenant base.</span></p></div><div><span &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black;background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Company\n law requires the directors to prepare financial statements for each financial\n year.<a></a> Under that law the directors have elected to prepare\n the financial statements in accordance<a></a> with United Kingdom\n Generally Accepted Accounting Practice (United Kingdom Accounting<a></a> Standards and applicable law). Under company law the\n directors must not approve the<a></a> financial statements unless\n they are satisfied that they give a true and fair view of the state of affairs\n of the company and of the profit or loss of the company for that period.<a></a> In preparing these financial statements, the directors are\n required to:</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA; Practice).</span><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">This report is made solely to the company's\nmembers, as a body, in accordance with Chapter 3<a></a> of Part 16\nof the Companies Act 2006.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Our audit\nwork has been undertaken so that we might<a></a> state to the\ncompany's members those matters we are required to state to them in an<a></a> auditor's report and for no other purpose.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>To the fullest extent permitted by law, we do<a></a> not accept or assume responsibility to anyone other than the\ncompany and the company's<a></a> members, as a body, for our audit\nwork, for this report, or for the opinions we have formed.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">As explained more fully in the Statement of\nDirectors' Responsibilities, the directors are<a></a> responsible\nfor the preparation of the financial statements and for being satisfied that<a></a> they give a true and fair view.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Our responsibility is to audit and express an\nopinion on<a></a> the financial statements in accordance with\napplicable law and International Standards on<a></a> Auditing (UK\nand Ireland).<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Those standards require us\nto comply with the Auditing<a></a> Practices Board's Ethical\nStandards for Auditors.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Scope of the audit of the\nfinancial statements</span></b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">An audit involves obtaining evidence about\nthe amounts and disclosures in the financial<a></a> statements\nsufficient to give reasonable assurance that the financial statements are free<a></a> from material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or\nerror.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This includes an assessment<a></a> of: whether the accounting policies are appropriate to the\ncompany's circumstances and have<a></a> been consistently applied\nand adequately disclosed; the reasonableness of significant<a></a>\naccounting estimates made by the directors; and the overall presentation of the\nfinancial<a></a> statements.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>In addition, we read all the financial and non-financial information in\nthe<a></a> annual report to identify material inconsistencies with\nthe audited financial statements. If we become aware of any apparent material\nmisstatements or inconsistencies we consider<a></a> the\nimplications for our report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Opinion on financial statements</span></b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><div><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns3:OpinionAuditorsOnEntity\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD_AUDITORS\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA; none;text-autospace:none\"><span class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA; none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA; style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:TurnoverPolicy\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\"><span style=\"background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Turnover represents rents\n receivable net of VAT and is recognised on an accruals basis in the period in\n which the rents become due.</span></ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:&#xD;&#xA;23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Investment properties</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:TangibleFixedAssetsPolicy\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD_INVESTMENT_PROPERTIES\"><span style=\"background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Investment properties are\n revalued annually and in accordance with SSAP 19 (Accounting for Investment\n Properties) no provision is made for depreciation. This departure from the\n requirements of the statutory accounting rules, which requires all properties\n to be depreciated is, in the opinion of the directors, necessary for the\n accounts to show a true and fair view. Depreciation is only one of the factors\n reflected in the annual valuation and the amount attributable to this factor\n is not capable of being separately identified or quantified. Surpluses or\n deficits are transferred to the revaluation reserve, unless a deficit exceeds\n previous surpluses recognised on the same property, in which case the excess\n is charged to the profit and loss account.</span></ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:&#xD;&#xA;23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Leases</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Rentals\npayable under operating leases are charged to the profit and loss account in\nthe period in which the rents become due.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Where\nlease incentives, including rent free periods, are received upon entering into\nthe lease, the benefit is recognised as an adjustment to rents payable\nallocated evenly over the lease term or the term to the first open market rent\nreview if earlier.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:&#xD;&#xA;23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade and other debtors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debtors\nare recognised initially at fair value.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>A provision for impairment is established where there is objective\nevidence that the company will not be able to collect all amounts due according\nto the original terms of the debtor concerned.</span></p></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div class=\"WordSection12\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:&#xD;&#xA;23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Taxation</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Current\ntax is provided at amounts expected to be paid or recovered using the tax rates\nand laws that have been enacted or substantively enacted at the balance sheet\ndate. The company is part of a UK group for group relief purposes and\naccordingly may take advantage of the group relief provisions whereby current\ntaxable profits can be offset by current tax losses arising in other companies\nin that group.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The group's policy is\nthat no payment will be made for tax losses surrendered under the group relief\nprovisions.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax assets and liabilities arise from timing differences between the\nrecognition of gains and losses in the financial statements and their\nrecognition in the corporation tax return.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Under\nFRS 19 deferred tax is recognised in respect of all timing differences that\nhave originated but not reversed at the balance sheet date where transactions\nor events that result in an obligation to pay more tax in the future or a right\nto pay less tax in the future have occurred at the balance sheet date.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>A net deferred tax asset is regarded as\nrecoverable and therefore recognised only when, on the basis of all available\nevidence, it can be regarded as more likely than not that there will be\nsuitable taxable profits from which the future reversal of the underlying\ntiming differences can be deducted.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is not recognised when fixed assets are revalued unless by the balance\nsheet date there is a binding agreement to sell the revalued assets and the\ngain or loss expected to arise on sale has been recognised in the financial\nstatements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is measured on a discounted basis to reflect the time value of money over\nthe period between the balance sheet date and the dates on which it is\nestimated that the timing differences will reverse, or where the timing\ndifferences are not expected to reverse, a period not exceeding 50 years.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Discount rates of 0.2% to 2.3% have been\nadopted reflecting the post-tax yield to maturity that can be obtained on\ngovernment bonds with similar maturity dates and currencies to those of the\ndeferred tax assets or liabilities.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:&#xD;&#xA;23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><a></a><b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">2.</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:&#xD;&#xA;1\">     </span><b>OPERATING PROFIT</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>None\nof the directors received any emoluments in respect of their services to the<a></a> company during the year or the prior year.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>No staff were employed by the company\nduring the year or the prior year.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Auditors'\nremuneration of £<span style=\"background:white;mso-highlight:white\">1,500</span>\n(2010: £500) for the audit of the company has been borne by another group\nundertaking.</span></p></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div class=\"WordSection13\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\"
